  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_9059790d-ee69-4ef3-a586-0a907576fc74'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<span id="freeTextContainer11031321899641269821">Bestseller book di Gramedia Bookstore selama 2 tahun berturut-turut!<br/><br/>Lima sahabat telah menjalin persahabatan selama tujuh tahun. Mereka adalah Arial yang paling tampan, Riani sebagai satu-satunya wanita dalam kelompok itu, Zafran yang berlagak seperti seorang penyair, Ian yang paling subur badannya, dan Genta yang dianggap sebagai leader dalam kelompok itu. Kegemaran merek</span>
  <span id="freeText11031321899641269821" style="display:none">Bestseller book di Gramedia Bookstore selama 2 tahun berturut-turut!<br /><br />Lima sahabat telah menjalin persahabatan selama tujuh tahun. Mereka adalah Arial yang paling tampan, Riani sebagai satu-satunya wanita dalam kelompok itu, Zafran yang berlagak seperti seorang penyair, Ian yang paling subur badannya, dan Genta yang dianggap sebagai leader dalam kelompok itu. Kegemaran mereka adalah mengeksekusi hal-hal yang tidak mungkin dan mencoba segala hal, mulai dari kafe paling terkenal di Jakarta, sampai nonton layar tancap. Semuanya penggemar film, dari film Hollywood sampai film yang nggak kelas—kecuali film India karena mereka punya prinsip bahwa semua persoalan di dunia atau masalah pasti ada jalan keluarnya, tapi bukan dalam bentuk joget.<br /><br />Suatu saat, karena terdorong oleh rasa bosan di antara satu dan yang lain, mereka memutuskan untuk tidak saling berkomunikasi dan bertemu satu sama lain selama tiga bulan. Selama tiga bulan berpisah itulah telah terjadi banyak hal yang membuat hati mereka lebih kaya dari sebelumnya. Pertemuan setelah tiga bulan yang penuh dengan rasa kangen akhirnya terjadi dan dirayakan dengan sebuah perjalanan. Sebuah perjalanan yang penuh dengan keyakinan, mimpi, cita-cita, dan cinta. Sebuah perjalanan yang telah mengubah mereka menjadi manusia sesungguhnya, bukan Cuma seonggok daging yang bisa berbicara, berjalan, dan punya nama.<br /><br /><i><b>“Ada yang pernah bilang kalau idealisme adalah kemewahan terakhir yang dimiliki oleh generasi muda….” </b> </i></span>

<div id="review_3400006314" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3400006314" />
    <a title="Ahmad" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/116665464-ahmad"><img alt="Ahmad" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3400006314?book_show_action=true">Jun 19, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ahmad" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ahmad" href="/user/show/116665464-ahmad">Ahmad</a>
      </span>

          added it




        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3400006314" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3409722768621536401">In my own thinking, this 5 cm book or novel is a book is very inspiring. It tells about Friendship, dreams, and lve that can change everything. Delivering with simple packaged but can be very beautiful. The somebody who likes traveling, nature , and adventure pshoild enjoy this plot of the novel. It provides the beutiful scenry of Mahameru Mountain and also bit ofBromo's view. However nothing is instant. Everything has a risk to be done and strugle. I have ever watched the film also and i deals </span>
  <span id="freeText3409722768621536401" style="display:none">In my own thinking, this 5 cm book or novel is a book is very inspiring. It tells about Friendship, dreams, and lve that can change everything. Delivering with simple packaged but can be very beautiful. The somebody who likes traveling, nature , and adventure pshoild enjoy this plot of the novel. It provides the beutiful scenry of Mahameru Mountain and also bit ofBromo's view. However nothing is instant. Everything has a risk to be done and strugle. I have ever watched the film also and i deals with my heroine on it. I never be sacrificed with only one sight.<br />In this 5cm novel describes the friendship of five human children named Arial, Riani, Zafran, Ian, and Genta. 5 person with 5 different personalities. The writer put each character on the one strong personality. Where they have their own obsessions and dreams. These five friends have been friends for seven years. One time they are bored with the activities they always do together. An idea for not communicating with each other and meeting each other for three months. The idea was proposed and all of them agreed. During the three months of separation, many things happened that made their hearts richer than before. The meeting after three months full of longing finally happened and celebrated with a wonderful trip.Along the way they discovered the true meaning of humanity. The journey full of meaning and value. All of them revealed in a trip 'reunion' they climbed the highest mountain on the island of Java, Mahameru.<br />On the way to Mahameru they experienced many events that they rarely saw in the city. In the climb they also get a lot of lessons for not giving up easily. Completing with the character name arial having a hypothermia. All of the member of the trip ever felt a doubt to continue the trip. But the problem was vanished because of their togetherness. The reader also fell in high spirit when 5 members on the 17th of August they celebrated Independence Day on the highest land in Java. However, before reaching the top, they had to climb the ocean of dust and rocks. Ian and other members had to strugle on it. Finally they made it. very touchy.<br />While the word '5 cm' means that we put our dream 5 cm in front of our forehead, don't just stick, let the dream hang, float 5 centimeters in front of your forehead, so the dream will never escape from your eyes. As close as your dream as well as it comes true.<br />The thing i like on this book are the interesting story, using language that is easy to understand, and the story line is not boring so the reader wants to read this book until the last page. The moral message delivered is so good that it motivates readers to be able to pursue their dreams and make them come true. Furthermore, i also can imagine the beutiful view that i want to discover.There are also lots of typical youth dialogues, but don't forget to add a touch of humor. <br />Poorly, there are also deficiencies in this novel. That is, too many song lyrics, which in my opinion, are very disturbing. There fore, it seems not to be useful to entertain the readers enough. Then,This novel iseems give the limit up to its target readers only for Indonesians. therefore, maybe foreign people will not be familiar with this story line. I suggest if there is a conflict that is more draining the reader's mind before leaving for train to Malang. for example like they did not go up the mountain for some reason or were given a surprise there was one of the member of them did not come along and it was already inside the train. I will give the good suprise for the readers and it will further make the reader more enthusiastic compared to displaying the ian almost get missed catch the train.</span>
  <a data-text-id="3409722768621536401" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_705805732" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/705805732" />
    <a title="Danan Wicaks" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13662847-danan-wicaks"><img alt="Danan Wicaks" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477186219p2/13662847.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/705805732?book_show_action=true">Aug 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Danan Wicaks" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Danan Wicaks" href="/user/show/13662847-danan-wicaks">Danan Wicaks</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer705805732" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer903151825965499931">How this book became best seller is beyond me. The narration is boring, repetitive, and too cliche. No symbolism, imagery and other literary devices are used by the author. There is no character development, they are exactly the same as from the start. In addition, the characters are also flat, too idealistic and have no flavor. Dialogues between characters are often meaningless and does not fit well with the flow of the story, makes you wonder whether it was a case of the author filling the pag</span>
  <span id="freeText903151825965499931" style="display:none">How this book became best seller is beyond me. The narration is boring, repetitive, and too cliche. No symbolism, imagery and other literary devices are used by the author. There is no character development, they are exactly the same as from the start. In addition, the characters are also flat, too idealistic and have no flavor. Dialogues between characters are often meaningless and does not fit well with the flow of the story, makes you wonder whether it was a case of the author filling the pages. But the worst part is the high number of typos in this book. Where was the editor?!<br /><br />It makes you think, if this book is best seller, what kind of youths with their stupid view of the ideal world (make no mistake, this book is a reflection of the wants of the average Indonesian youth) and their lack of literary appreciation will bring this country out of its backside?<br /><br />There are some good themes about friendship, dreams, and attempts to glorify nationalism. But the bottom line is, if this is the literary marvel Indonesia has to offer today, then the our modern culture is in a sad, sad state.</span>
  <a data-text-id="903151825965499931" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2378222293" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1031066965046784989">"MEGA BESTSELLER" was written at the corner of the book's cover and the review at the back cover basically said that the book was very very good, plus it has a really cool cover, so I thought it would worth reading.<br/><br/>I did not bother to read the first chapter where the author introduced each of the characters. Readers should be able to find out more about a character through the story, after all, not through a detailed description at the beginning of the story. It was actually a turn off for me, b</span>
  <span id="freeText1031066965046784989" style="display:none">"MEGA BESTSELLER" was written at the corner of the book's cover and the review at the back cover basically said that the book was very very good, plus it has a really cool cover, so I thought it would worth reading.<br /><br />I did not bother to read the first chapter where the author introduced each of the characters. Readers should be able to find out more about a character through the story, after all, not through a detailed description at the beginning of the story. It was actually a turn off for me, but I kept reading. The story would have progressed faster if the author did not throw in songs and famous people's quotes here and there and just get into the main point. The first few chapters felt more like a filler to me (the five friends cutting contact off and all). The book's about the friends going on a hike all along, but the author just took a roundabout way to get to it. I ended up skipping the rest of the book and went straight to the ending.<br /><br />Though there is one thing that I like: hang your dreams 5 cm in front of your forehead so that you can always see it and keep on chasing after it.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1031066965046784989" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1422594930" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1422594930" />
    <a title="Faza Subandrio" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47211583-faza-subandrio"><img alt="Faza Subandrio" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1422594930?book_show_action=true">Oct 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Faza Subandrio" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Faza Subandrio" href="/user/show/47211583-faza-subandrio">Faza Subandrio</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1422594930" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14878835490025170993">The story is about five friends who have been friends for seven years. There are: Genta, who considered as the leader of their friendship. Zafran, the artsy-kind-of-guy that in the future, he wants to be a famous poet. Riani, the only female friend in that group who has a bubbly personality. Arial, the most handsome guy in the group, who shares the same font name “Arial”, which is the font that I’m typing right now, it is because he has a bold body, get it ? And last but not least, there is Ian.</span>
  <span id="freeText14878835490025170993" style="display:none">The story is about five friends who have been friends for seven years. There are: Genta, who considered as the leader of their friendship. Zafran, the artsy-kind-of-guy that in the future, he wants to be a famous poet. Riani, the only female friend in that group who has a bubbly personality. Arial, the most handsome guy in the group, who shares the same font name “Arial”, which is the font that I’m typing right now, it is because he has a bold body, get it ? And last but not least, there is Ian. The chubbiest guy in the group, who is a football maniac, and avid fan of various “blue” film.<br /><br />One day, triggered by their boredom between one and the other, they decided not to communicate for three months. Parted for three months period, there are much things that going on makes their hearts feel fulfilled than before. After the three months of “We’re-Not-Going-To-Communicate-For-Three-Months-Because-We-Are-Bored.” That kind of thing, they celebrated their parted-ways-thing with a field trip.<br /><br />Okay, enough revealing the plot, let’s get down to the review!<br />I’m going to write it down as good as I can, it’s because I sucked at reviewing books. But not comic books, though!<br /><br />Review:<br />The young adult story about friendship for over seven years is the rarest and little bit unrealistic. The rare thing is, when I read it, they shared the same interest(s). For example: Music and film (In the novel). Now, this is the rarest thing that will happens for certain people, like me!<br /> For instance, I like comic books because my brother in his college years, left me some Indonesian-translated comic books that can you found on certain used-books store today. I read it comics to comics, characters to characters, until the certain comic company made a movie(s) about it.<br />When you found one of a person who likes it. Sometimes you compared, debated, and favorited who has the same interested as you. Gradually, you became friends, or, the best case scenario, when you have opposite gender who has same interest as you, same as I mentioned above, you became friends, then you start dating him/her, and then live happily ever after. That is an uncut diamond, people! Because it’s rare to have friendship like that.<br /><br />	. Friend(s) come and go, because time is not on our side. However, the unrealistic part of a friendship is, from my experience, my duration being a friend only lasted for about two to three years. As the novel told the story, their friendship is still intact for seven years old and still counting. I don’t know how they do it, but they have magic of their own. But for me, I began my introversion on my junior high years, it is because some of them are hard for me to adapt for having minimum same interest(s) as me. My phase two of the introversion has been developed in my high school year, where people has barely has the same interest as me.<br />	<br />	But, some people make friends by only shows your existential to the people who wants to be popular on your schools. Don’t be like that<br /> <br />In most humble opinion, in this novel, on the friendship part, it taught me you don’t have to do anything only just want your name to have a reputation. You just have to show you who really are underneath the mask, and let someone can accept your imperfection. Because the world is an imperfect place.<br /><br />Overall, 10/10 would read it again. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="14878835490025170993" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4472713-nur-fadilla-octavianasari?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4472713-nur-fadilla-octavianasari?shelf=borrowed-rented">borrowed-rented</a>,

              <span id="reviewTextContainer144163753" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9033966418221766209">I'm sure some of you have read this book. I myself can say it is too late for me to read it. I just read the book about on November last year, whereas the book was published in 2005. But, I think late is better than never right? By the way thanks to Annisa who’s borrowing me this inspirational book.<br/><br/>5 cm a book by Donny Dhirgantoro begin with the friendship between five peoples named Arial, Riani, Zafran, Ian, and Genta. Hang out, nights weekly and empty time spent together. Because so often toge</span>
  <span id="freeText9033966418221766209" style="display:none">I'm sure some of you have read this book. I myself can say it is too late for me to read it. I just read the book about on November last year, whereas the book was published in 2005. But, I think late is better than never right? By the way thanks to Annisa who’s borrowing me this inspirational book.<br /><br />5 cm a book by Donny Dhirgantoro begin with the friendship between five peoples named Arial, Riani, Zafran, Ian, and Genta. Hang out, nights weekly and empty time spent together. Because so often together, they feel they need to have time to not communicate and meet each other for three month. Various interesting things happening for 3 months. Thesis, relationship, internship and other spectacular things. After three months the meeting finally happened and celebrated with a trip to Semeru Mountain.<br /> <br />5 cm is a book with full of inspiration, passion, and various small example how life is really beautiful. The strength of this book is there are a lot of valuable quotations. I often heard the quote "The best people are benefit for others." Not just a piece of meat that can talk, walk, and had a name. But they can ultimately reaching their dreams that they dream long ago.<br /><br />In my opinion, the climax of passion and reflection of life in this book there is on Deniek letter to Adrian. In this context, I could really absorb the meaning of the word "The best people are benefit for others." Emotions are very strong in the letter. Climax sequel is where Ian was not aware for some time. Zafran was screaming. Riani cry. The ending climax when they reached the top of Mahameru and follow the flag ceremony on August 17. <br /><br />Title 5 cm itself is about the spirit of reaching a dream. <br />"... Let your confidence, 5 centimeters hung and floating in front of you. After that all you need just foot that will go further than usual, the hands that will do more than usual, eyes that will stare longer than usual, the neck that will more often look up. Layer of intentions that a thousand times harder than steel, a heart that will work harder than normal and the mouth that will always pray ... believe in the 5 centimeters in front of your forehead”<br /><br />No dream is too high and so forth. 5 cm perfecting my belief that all dreams can be achieved. Nothing is impossible, as long as we keep the spirit, trying and trying. <br />Let’s make our dream list, and try to reach it. Congratulations to reach the dream, man. We can make it.<br /></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer712718759151494212">I rarely find Indonesian novel that is as good as this (probably not too much Indonesian novel I read). These are several of my comments:<br/><br/>1. This book is a daily life book that is really familiar with real life (although still it's too perfect if compared with real 'real life'). At least there is no such surprising event, dramatic moment, etc. Everything is very normal, down to earth, and very honest. That's why I love it<br/><br/>2. The story also has very good theme: about dream and how to reach it, very</span>
  <span id="freeText712718759151494212" style="display:none">I rarely find Indonesian novel that is as good as this (probably not too much Indonesian novel I read). These are several of my comments:<br /><br />1. This book is a daily life book that is really familiar with real life (although still it's too perfect if compared with real 'real life'). At least there is no such surprising event, dramatic moment, etc. Everything is very normal, down to earth, and very honest. That's why I love it<br /><br />2. The story also has very good theme: about dream and how to reach it, very suitable to be read by youngster these days.<br /><br />3. I plan to hike Bromo mountain some time next year. After reading this book I realize that it's not going to be easy, but I am really challenged to do it. Some parts like stones fall down from above is somehow seems over told, but I don't know, it probably happens in active mountain. Well I will never know until I experience it by myself.<br /><br />4. It contains full of: Song's lyrics (I am not a music lover, so I skip it a lot), great man's quote (this one I am really like, and actually some quotes are really inspiring) <br /><br />5. I read the comic book version before this. Now I know that the novel version more colorful and give stronger picture of each character, the plot and the setting. I am glad to re-read the novel version.<br /><br />Hope I can find this qualified book next time !!!</span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer289366680" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11378190201480759660">nice cover and catchy title. but 5cm failed to impress me further. the story is linear.. about a group of young friends and met again after separated for 3 months and went on an amazing reunion adventure of climbing the "mahameru" (The highest mountain in java-Indonesia). at first it was a flat pace rather slow.. but things get quite interesting as they separated, before entering the linear pace when they started the mahameru journey.<br/>The story might appeal on readers who have experienced the "re</span>
  <span id="freeText11378190201480759660" style="display:none">nice cover and catchy title. but 5cm failed to impress me further. the story is linear.. about a group of young friends and met again after separated for 3 months and went on an amazing reunion adventure of climbing the "mahameru" (The highest mountain in java-Indonesia). at first it was a flat pace rather slow.. but things get quite interesting as they separated, before entering the linear pace when they started the mahameru journey.<br />The story might appeal on readers who have experienced the "real" mountain climbing activites. But a lack of twist and surprises in the story will reduced the "emotional attachment" on regular readers. <br />i'm a music lover with a top-40-ears. but the amount of songs that were quote and lyrics written in this book is on an annoying level for me. i always skip the lyrics parts and continue with the story.<br />and i personally think that this book do not represent the real youngsters as intended. too much psychic and telekinetic power between these 5 friends. they seems to be able to read what others are thinking and-heck, even what they are trying to say!? on the otherhand as being described in the prologue.. each character have a very different character between each other. how could a lunatic artist befriended and have "telekinetic" power with a gym-junkie-metrosexual-prodigy?? highly unreal for me...</span>

  <span id="freeText12377624813415153688" style="display:none">When I first read it, I thought it was a story about best friends who go through some kind of change in their friendship. But it wasn't. The plot was unclear and jumps from one plot to another. The style of writing and the point of the story - if you can call it a story at all - simply do not go with one another. Also, the characterising of the characters wasn't made clear and real. It was as if all the characters were one entity. Yeah, sure, they split up for a bit but even then there isn't much of the characters to be seen. It's as if they don't have individualism. And how strange that at such an age, after going through a lot, that they have never seen anyone else. Don't they have friends of their own, each and every one of them? The whole book just makes me feel like nothing is real, it's no different from reading a school book about how you should behave with empathy and kindness. Except it would've been more straight forward.</span>

<div class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground">Readers also enjoyed</h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent"><div class='bookCarousel'>
<div class='carouselRow' style='width: 3600px'>
<ul>
<li class='cover' id='bookCover_6765740'>
<a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/6765740-perahu-kertas"><img alt="Perahu Kertas" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/books/1356225544l/6765740._SX98_.jpg" />
</a>

  
<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('EbFOMVNEKEMHBnL0ZqmgmKGVgkedN4UPzub5R/6UZoIHdUiV7+dX4lKvYCuYVUDgu8GLkIYYqVviUzGwT8FIvQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Z+GR4X+eDQn2Yl31vRmR2dUxfBybiae1zNit0iZsyRRxJZdFwz1yqKPLTypD5XGhz2V1y4Cmi+HgbWUllznnKw==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
